{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01NKWkELSexJo67nHbvT1Lfs","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"thinking","thinking":"Looking at the code, I can see that in `file.go`, line 115-121, when a remote registry is accessed, the code does:\n\n```go\nif s.opts.auth != nil {\n    remote.Client = &auth.Client{\n        Credential: s.opts.auth(ref.Registry),\n        Cache:      auth.DefaultCache,\n        Client:     retry.DefaultClient,\n    }\n}\n```\n\nThe `Credential` is set from `s.opts.auth(ref.Registry)` which is a `credentialFunc` (defined on line 40 as `func(registry string) auth.CredentialFunc`).\n\nThe current ECR implementation has a `Credential` method that fetches the token once. The issue is that this token is cached by the ORAS library and never refreshed. AWS ECR authorization tokens expire after approximately 12 hours\n2. The ORAS library caches credentials but doesn't respect token expiry\n3. After expiry, bundle pulls would fail until credentials were manually rotated\n\n## Solution Overview\nImplemented automatic token refresh with TTL-aware credential caching in the AWS ECR provider.\n\n## Changes Made\n\n### 1. **Modified `internal/oci/ecr/ecr.go`**\n\n#### Added Structures:\n- `cachedCredential`: Stores credentials with their expiry time\n- Extended `ECR` struct with:\n  - `mu sync.Mutex`: Thread-safe credential access\n  - `cachedCredential`: Cached credential with expiry\n  - `refreshBufferTime`: Configurable buffer before token expiry\n\n#### Key Methods:\n- `NewECR()`: Constructor that initializes with 5-minute refresh buffer\n- `Credential()`: Main method that:\n  - Checks if cached credential is still valid\n  - Fetches fresh token if expired or about to expire\n  - Returns cached credential if still valid\n  - Thread-safe with mutex protection\n- `fetchCredentialWithExpiry()`: Fetches token and extracts expiry time from AWS ECR response\n- `fetchCredential()`: Wrapper for backward compatibility\n\n#### Features:\n- Tokens are refreshed 5 minutes before actual expiry (safety buffer)\n- Uses AWS SDK's credentials chain for authentication\n- Extracts `ExpiresAt` field from ECR authorization response\n- Default refresh buffer is 5 minutes if not specified\n\n### 2. **Modified `internal/oci/options.go`**\n- Updated `WithAWSECRCredentials()` to use `ecr.NewECR()` constructor\n- Added clarifying documentation about automatic token refresh\n\n### 3. **Added Comprehensive Tests in `internal/oci/ecr/ecr_test.go`**\n- Test credential caching when not expired\n- Test token refresh when approaching expiry\n- Test refresh buffer time boundary conditions\n- Test zero-value ECR instance with default buffer\n- All tests verify correct fetch/cache behavior\n\n## Configuration\nUsers can enable AWS ECR authentication with:\n\n```yaml\nstorage:\n  type: oci\n  oci:\n    repository: my-registry.dkr.ecr.us-east-1.amazonaws.com/my-bundle:latest\n    authentication:\n      type: aws-ecr  # Uses AWS credentials chain\n```\n\nOr via environment:\n```bash\nFLIPT_STORAGE_TYPE=oci\nFLIPT_STORAGE_OCI_REPOSITORY=my-registry.dkr.ecr.us-east-1.amazonaws.com/my-bundle:latest\nFLIPT_STORAGE_OCI_AUTHENTICATION_TYPE=aws-ecr\n```\n\n## How It Works\n\n1. When Flipt needs to pull bundles from ECR, it calls the `Credential()` method\n2. The method checks if a cached credential exists and is still valid (not within 5 minutes of expiry)\n3. If valid, the cached credential is returned immediately\n4. If expired or approaching expiry, a fresh token is fetched using AWS credentials chain\n5. The new token is cached with its expiry time\n6. Future credential requests use the cached token until it's about to expire\n\n## Benefits\n\n- **Automatic Refresh**: Tokens are refreshed before expiry without manual intervention\n- **Continuous Syncing**: Bundle syncing continues across token expiries\n- **AWS Credentials Chain**: Supports all AWS credential providers (env vars, IAM roles, etc.)\n- **Thread-Safe**: Uses mutex to ensure concurrent access is safe\n- **Configurable**: Refresh buffer time can be customized if needed\n- **Backward Compatible**: Existing code continues to work without changes\n\n## Test Results\n- All OCI tests pass ✓\n- All ECR tests pass ✓\n- All config tests pass ✓\n- All storage tests pass ✓\n- New caching tests verify token refresh behavior ✓\nEOF\ncat /tmp/IMPLEMENTATION_SUMMARY.md\n","description":"Create implementation summary"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":0,"cache_creation_input_tokens":280,"cache_read_input_tokens":101170,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":280},"output_tokens":5,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"3e94e52f-60e7-4eac-842e-89394c9ecd92","uuid":"d363ac34-4039-4740-8f74-9461c0cfb15b"}
